## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / mathematical biology (population dynamics)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is the time-derivative of population size P, a standard setup for continuous-time population dynamics in ecology. Typical models express dP_dt as intrinsic growth minus density-dependent limitation, external forcing in time t, and/or removals such as harvesting.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Malthusian (exponential) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited resources, constant per-capita growth)
- Constant immigration/emigration: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (net influx/outflux independent of P)
- Linear density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 (crowding reduces per-capita growth approximately linearly in P)
- Verhulst / logistic ODE form: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P) (carrying-capacity-type self-limitation; typically c1 < 0)
- Theta-logistic (generalized density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P**c2) (flexible curvature of density dependence via exponent c2)
- Gompertz-type growth (log-density regulation): dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 * P) (per-capita growth decreases ~log(P); c1 sets scale)
- Allee effect (depensation): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P) * (c2 * P + c3) (growth depressed at low P; parameters set threshold and carrying effects)
- Saturating per-capita growth (crowding-limited reproduction): dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (birth process saturates with density)
- Time-varying intrinsic rate (trend): dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P (gradual environmental change in growth rate)
- Seasonal forcing (periodic environment): dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P (seasonal variation in per-capita growth)
- Pulsed/decaying environmental influence: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) * P (transient change in growth rate over time)
- Harvesting/removal: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (constant-yield harvesting if c1 < 0) or dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P (proportional harvesting if c1 < 0)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Per-capita growth representation: if dP_dt is proportional to P (i.e., dP_dt/P depends on t or P), models often take the form dP_dt = P * g(t, P).
- Density dependence via curvature: adding higher powers of P (e.g., P**2, P**c) typically encodes stronger-than-linear crowding and changing stability near equilibria.
- Carrying capacity as a root: forms where dP_dt includes a factor (1 + c*P) imply an equilibrium at P = -1/c and sign-change around that point.
- Allee threshold as a root at low P: an additional factor (c2*P + c3) creates a low-density equilibrium/threshold below which growth becomes negative.
- Log-regulation signature: terms like P*log(c*P) indicate multiplicative growth in P with regulation acting on log-density (often smoother approach to equilibrium).
- Seasonality/forcing: sin(c*t + phase) multiplying P typically produces oscillations in growth rate without requiring P to oscillate sinusoidally.
- Harvesting detection: additive negative terms (approximately constant in P) suggest constant-yield removal; multiplicative negative terms in P suggest proportional removal.
- Saturation in crowding-limited processes: rational forms P/(1 + c*P) imply diminishing returns in dP_dt as P increases, consistent with limited reproduction/space.

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG6)
============================================================
GT: -c0*c1*P + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P**c6 + c7*P
Candidate formulas: 50

Let’s first simplify the Ground Truth (GT) into a standard polynomial-in-\(P\) plus a \(P^{1/3}\) term.

### 0) Ground Truth simplification
GT:
\[
- c0c1 P + c2(c3 - P/c4)P + c5 P^{c6} + c7 P
\]
With given values \(c3=1\), \(c6=\tfrac13\), and \(c2=c5=c7=0.8578822735\):
\[
= (-c0c1)P + c2(P - P^2/c4) + c5 P^{1/3} + c7 P
\]
Group like terms:
- \(P^2\) coefficient: \(-c2/c4\)
- \(P\) coefficient: \(-c0c1 + c2 + c7\)
- \(P^{1/3}\) coefficient: \(c5\)
- constant term: \(0\)
- no \(t\) dependence

Numerically:
- \(P^{1/3}\) coefficient \(= 0.8578822735168387\)
- \(P^2\) coefficient \(= -0.8578822735168387 / 79.20259671838578\) (some fixed negative number)
- \(P\) coefficient \(= -6.216849410245645\cdot 1.4127513976416965 + 0.8578822735168387 + 0.8578822735168387\) (some fixed number)
So GT has the exact form:
\[
\text{GT}(P,t)= A\,P^{1/3} + B\,P^2 + C\,P
\]
with fixed constants \(A,B,C\), and **no** \(t\), **no** constant offset, **no** piecewise terms.

Therefore, any candidate can match iff it can be reduced (by choosing its constants) to exactly \(A P^{1/3} + B P^2 + C P\) for all real \(P\) (and all \(t\), though GT ignores \(t\)).

---

## Candidate-by-candidate analysis

### 1. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^{1/3}c1 + P^2c2 + Pc3 + c4\max(0,-P+c5)\)
The \(\max\) term is piecewise and cannot equal 0 for all \(P\) unless its coefficient is 0. Set \(c4=0\). Then expression becomes:
\[
(c0+c1)P^{1/3} + c2 P^2 + c3 P
\]
This matches GT by choosing:
- \(c2 = B\)
- \(c3 = C\)
- \(c0+c1 = A\)
So **matches**.

### 2. Candidate 1 plus \(c6\max(0,P+c7)\)
Set both piecewise coefficients to zero: \(c4=0, c6=0\). Reduces to same as (1), so **matches**.

### 3. Candidate 2 plus another \(\max(0,P+c9)\)
Set \(c4=0, c6=0, c8=0\). Reduces to same core polynomial, so **matches**.

### 4. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^2c1 + Pc2 + Pc3 + Pc4 + c5\sin(Pc6+c7)+c8\)
To match GT, must remove sine and constant: set \(c5=0\), \(c8=0\).
Then:
\[
c0 P^{1/3} + c1 P^2 + (c2+c3+c4)P
\]
Choose \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\), \(c2+c3+c4=C\). **Matches**.

### 5. Includes \(c4|P|\), \(t\) terms, and constant
GT has no \(|P|\), no \(t\), no constant. Set \(c4=0\). For \(t\): expression has \(c5 t + c7 t + t = (c5+c7+1)t\); must be 0 for all \(t\), so choose \(c5+c7+1=0\). Constant term \(c6\) must be 0. Then remaining \(P\)-part is:
\[
c0P^{1/3} + c1P^2 + (c2+c3+c4?)P
\]
Here \(c4\) already set 0; so linear coefficient \(c2+c3\). Choose to match \(A,B,C\). **Matches**.

### 6. Similar to 5 with \(|P|\), constant, and \(c6 t + t\)
Set \(|P|\) coefficient \(c4=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c6+1=0\). Remove constant: \(c5=0\). Then match remaining coefficients. **Matches**.

### 7. Has constant \(c5\) and \(c6 t + t\)
Set \(c5=0\), and \(c6+1=0\) to remove \(t\). Then match \(P^{1/3},P^2,P\) via \(c0,c1,(c2+c3+c4)\). **Matches**.

### 8. Many \(P^2\), many \(P\), constant, and \(t\)
Set constant \(c8=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c9+1=0\). Combine terms:
- \(P^{1/3}\): \(c0\)
- \(P^2\): \(c1+c2+c3\)
- \(P\): \(c4+c5+c6+c7\)
Choose sums to equal \(A,B,C\). **Matches**.

### 9. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^{1/3} + P^2c1 + Pc2 + c3\max(0,-P+c4)\)
Need remove max: set \(c3=0\). Then \(P^{1/3}\) coefficient is \(c0+1\), adjustable to any real by choosing \(c0=A-1\). Set \(c1=B\), \(c2=C\). **Matches**.

### 10. Has \(c7 t + t\)
Remove \(t\): \(c7+1=0\). Then match sums of \(P^2\) and \(P\) coefficients and \(P^{1/3}\) via \(c0\). **Matches**.

### 11. Has \(t\) and a max term
Set max coefficient \(c8=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c7+1=0\). Then match polynomial coefficients. **Matches**.

### 12. Has \(+P\) fixed and constant \(c3\), and \(c4 t + t\)
Remove \(t\): \(c4+1=0\). Remove constant: \(c3=0\). Linear term is \(c2 P + P = (c2+1)P\), adjustable. Set \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\), \(c2=C-1\). **Matches**.

### 13. Has \(|P|\), constants, and \(t\)
Set \(|P|\) coefficient \(c6=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c7+c9+1=0\). Remove constant: \(c8=0\). Then match remaining coefficients (note multiple \(P\) terms). **Matches**.

### 14. Many \(P^2\), many \(P\), and \(t\)
Remove \(t\): \(c9+1=0\). Then match \(c0=A\), sum of \(P^2\) coefficients \(=B\), sum of \(P\) coefficients \(=C\). **Matches**.

### 15. Has \(c5 t\) and constant \(c6\)
Remove \(t\): \(c5=0\). Remove constant: \(c6=0\). Then match \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\), and \(c2+c3+c4=C\). **Matches**.

### 16. Two max terms
Set both max coefficients to zero: \(c3=0, c5=0\). Then it’s \(c0P^{1/3}+c1P^2+c2P\). Match directly. **Matches**.

### 17. Has \(|P|\) and \(t\)
Set \(|P|\) coefficient \(c4=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c5+c7=0\). Remove constant: \(c6=0\). Then match remaining coefficients. **Matches**.

### 18. Has constant and \(t\)
Set constant \(c5=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c6+c7=0\). Then match \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\), and \(c2+c3+c4=C\). **Matches**.

### 19. Has \(c4 t + t\)
Remove \(t\): \(c4+1=0\). Then match \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\), and \(c2+c3=C\). **Matches**.

### 20. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P^{1/3}c1 + P^2c2 + Pc3\)
Already exactly the GT functional form. Choose \(c0+c1=A\), \(c2=B\), \(c3=C\). **Matches**.

### 21. Candidate 20 plus \(c4\max(0,-P)\)
Set \(c4=0\). Then same as 20. **Matches**.

### 22. Has a fixed \(+P^2\) and \(t\)
Remove \(t\): \(c6+1=0\). Then \(P^2\) coefficient is \(c1+c2+1\), adjustable to \(B\). Linear coefficient sum adjustable to \(C\). \(c0=A\). **Matches**.

### 23. Has constant \(c4\) and \(c5 t + t\)
Remove constant: \(c4=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c5+1=0\). Then match remaining coefficients. **Matches**.

### 24. Has constant and \(t\)
Remove constant: \(c6=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c7+c8=0\). Then match coefficients. **Matches**.

### 25. Has \(c6 t + t\)
Remove \(t\): \(c6+1=0\). Then match sums for \(P^2\) and \(P\), and \(c0=A\). **Matches**.

### 26. Has fixed \(+P\), constant, and \(t\)
Remove constant: \(c4=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c5+c6=0\). Linear coefficient is \(c2+c3+1\), adjustable to \(C\). Match \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\). **Matches**.

### 27. Has max term
Set max coefficient \(c5=0\). Then match \(c0=A\), \(c1+c2=B\), \(c3+c4=C\). **Matches**.

### 28. Has max and an exp(t)*max term
Set both nonlinear add-ons to zero: \(c5=0\) and \(c7=0\). Then same as 27 without extras. **Matches**.

### 29. Has extra \(P/(c4+t)^5\) term
To match GT (no \(t\)-dependence), must eliminate that term. But it has no multiplicative free coefficient; it is fixed as \(+ P/(c4+t)^5\). There is no way to make it identically zero for all \(P,t\) by choosing \(c4\). So **cannot match**.

### 30. Has \(|P|\), constant, and \(c6 t + 2t\)
Remove \(|P|\): \(c4=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c6+2=0\). Remove constant: \(c5=0\). Then match remaining coefficients. **Matches**.

### 31. Has max term
Set \(c3=0\). Then match \(c0=A\), \(c1=B\), \(c2=C\). **Matches**.

### 32. Has max and exp(t)*max
Set \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then match polynomial. **Matches**.

### 33. Has max term
Set max coefficient \(c5=0\). Then expression is \(c0P^{1/3}+c1P^2+c2P^2+c3P+c4P\). Choose \(c0=A\), \(c1+c2=B\), \(c3+c4=C\). **Matches**.

### 34. Has rational-in-\(t\) terms and a max term
The term \(\max(0,P+c8)\) has fixed coefficient 1 (not removable). No choice of \(c8\) makes \(\max(0,P+c8)\) identically zero for all \(P\). Therefore cannot equal GT for all \(P\). **Cannot match**.

### 35. Has constant and \(c7 t + t\)
Remove constant: \(c6=0\). Remove \(t\): \(c7+1=0\). Then match coefficients. **Matches**.
